                                        <script>\n                            var swap_on=false;\n                            var swap_time_out;\n                            var state_txt_animado=0;\n                            function startSwapTextos(){\n                                if(swap_on==false){\n                                    swapAlertFestivos();\n                                    swap_on=true;\n                                }\n                            }\n                            function stopSwapTextos(){\n                                if(swap_on==true){\n                                    cancelswapAlertFestivos();\n                                    swap_on=false;\n                                }\n                            }\n                            function swapAlertFestivos(){\n                                if(state_txt_animado==0){\n                                    swapShowEnvio();\n                                    state_txt_animado=1;\n                                }\n                                else{\n                                    swapShowAlertTienda();\n                                    state_txt_animado=0;\n                                }\n                                swap_time_out=setTimeout(function(){swapAlertFestivos();},30000);\n                            }\n                            function swapShowEnvio(){\n                                $(\"#swap_textos_envio\").show();\n                                $(\"#swap_alerta_festivos\").hide();\n                            }\n                            function swapShowAlertTienda(){\n                                $(\"#swap_textos_envio\").hide();\n                                    $(\"#swap_alerta_festivos\").show();\n                            }\n                            function cancelswapAlertFestivos(){\n                                clearTimeout(swap_time_out);\n                                swapShowEnvio();\n                                state_txt_animado=0;\n                            }\n                        </script>\n                        <div
